<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доверить.html>дове́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dovéritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доверительный.html>довери́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">doverítelʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)довери́тельнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)довери́тельней</b>)

<li>trusting, confiding</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> warrant, power of attorney; trust, confidence</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:доверить.html>дове́рить</a> (7589)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верить.html>ве́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">véritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доверить.html>дове́рить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dovéritʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доверять.html>доверя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to entrust (to)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:доверить.html>дове́рить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тайна.html>та́йны</a> кому́-либо</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovéritʹ</b> svoí tájny komú-libo</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to take somebody into one's confidence</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***доверчивость.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:доверчивость.html>дове́рчивость</a> (17272)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доверчивый.html>дове́рчивый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dovérčivyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доверчивость.html>дове́рчивость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dovérčivostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доверчивость.html>дове́рчивости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доверчивость.html>дове́рчивости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доверчивость.html>дове́рчивостей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>trustfulness</li>
<li>credulity</li>
<li>gullibility (quality of being easily deceived)</li></ol>

***довести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>довести́</a> (3083)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>довести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dovestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lead, to take, to accompany <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to bring <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">into</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>довести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дому́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovestí</b> do domú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to see (someone) home</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cooking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to scald
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>довести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кипение.html>кипе́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovestí</b> do kipénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to scald</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to drive, to reduce, to bring, to carry
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>довести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:изнеможение.html>изнеможе́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovestí</b> do iznemožénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tire out</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>довести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:беда.html>беды́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovestí</b> do bedý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lead to trouble</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>довести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нищета.html>нищеты́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovestí</b> do niščetý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reduce to poverty</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>довести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчаяние.html>отча́яния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovestí</b> do otčájanija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drive to despair</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>довести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слеза.html>слёз</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovestí</b> do sljóz</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drive to tears, to make cry</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>довести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершенство.html>соверше́нства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovestí</b> do soveršénstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to perfect, to bring to perfection</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>довести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сумасшествие.html>сумасше́ствия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovestí</b> do sumasšéstvija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drive crazy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>довести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>конца́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovestí</b> do koncá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to carry through, to carry to conclusion, to complete</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>довести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крайность.html>кра́йности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovestí</b> do krájnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to push too far, to drive over the edge, to take to extremes, to carry to an extreme</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to inform
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>довести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сознание.html>созна́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovestí</b> do soznánija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring home to</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>довести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сведение.html>све́дения</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovestí</b> do svédenija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to inform</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***доводить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a> (7488)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dovodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:довести.html>довести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to see, to lead, to take, to accompany <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to bring <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">into</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дому́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovodítʹ</b> do domú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to see home</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cooking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to scald
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кипение.html>кипе́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovodítʹ</b> do kipénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to scald</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to drive, to reduce, to bring, to carry
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:изнеможение.html>изнеможе́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovodítʹ</b> do iznemožénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tire out</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:беда.html>беды́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovodítʹ</b> do bedý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lead to trouble</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нищета.html>нищеты́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovodítʹ</b> do niščetý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reduce to poverty</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчаяние.html>отча́яния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovodítʹ</b> do otčájanija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drive to despair</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слеза.html>слёз</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovodítʹ</b> do sljóz</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drive to tears, to make cry</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершенство.html>соверше́нства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovodítʹ</b> do soveršénstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to perfect, to bring to perfection</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сумасшествие.html>сумасше́ствия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovodítʹ</b> do sumasšéstvija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drive crazy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>конца́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovodítʹ</b> do koncá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to carry through, to carry to conclusion, to complete</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крайность.html>кра́йности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovodítʹ</b> do krájnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to push too far, to drive over the edge, to take to extremes, to carry to an extreme</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to inform
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сознание.html>созна́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovodítʹ</b> do soznánija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring home to</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сведение.html>све́дения</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dovodítʹ</b> do svédenija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to inform</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:доводиться.html>доводи́ться</a> (9468)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dovodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доводиться.html>доводи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dovodítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:довестись.html>довести́сь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to have an occasion <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to happen <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be related to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:доводиться.html>дово́дится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дядя.html>дя́дей</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:брат.html>бра́том</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on mne <b>dovóditsja</b> djádej (brátom)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is my uncle (brother)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>ке́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:доводиться.html>дово́дится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщина</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kem vam <b>dovóditsja</b> éta žénščina?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">how are you related to this woman?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доводить.html>доводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dovodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***довольство.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:довольство.html>дово́льство</a> (20520)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дово́ль(ный)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dovólʹ(nyj)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:довольство.html>дово́льство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dovólʹstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:довольство.html>дово́льства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:довольство.html>дово́льства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:довольство.html>дово́льств</a></b>)

***догадаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:догадаться.html>догада́ться</a> (1521)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гадать.html>гада́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gadátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:догадаться.html>догада́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dogadátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:догадываться.html>дога́дываться</a></b>) (<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + prepositional case)
</p>
<ol><li>to guess <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to reach an unqualified conclusion</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to surmise, to suspect, to conjecture</li>
<li>to cotton on, to glom on</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угадать.html>угада́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ugadátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to guess, transitive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***догадливый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:догадливый.html>дога́дливый</a> (19725)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">догада́ть(ся)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dogadátʹ(sja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ливый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-livyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:догадливый.html>дога́дливый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dogádlivyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>quick-witted, clever</li></ol>

***догадываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:догадываться.html>дога́дываться</a> (2524)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:догадаться.html>догада́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dogadátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:догадываться.html>дога́дываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dogádyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:догадаться.html>догада́ться</a></b>) (<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + prepositional case)
</p>
<ol><li>to guess <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to reach an unqualified conclusion</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to surmise, to suspect, to conjecture</li></ol>

***догнать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:догнать.html>догна́ть</a> (2982)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнать.html>гнать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gnatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:догнать.html>догна́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dognátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:догонять.html>догоня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to catch up, to overtake</li>
<li>to drive to, to bring to</li></ol>
